\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{vector_8c_source_l03956}03956     \textcolor{comment}{// To store the answer}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{vector_8c_source_l03957}03957     \textcolor{keywordtype}{long} \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} ans = 0.;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{vector_8c_source_l03958}03958     \textcolor{comment}{// To find integral part of square}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{vector_8c_source_l03959}03959     \textcolor{comment}{// root of number}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{vector_8c_source_l03960}03960     \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (start <= end) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{vector_8c_source_l03961}03961         \textcolor{comment}{// Find mid}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{vector_8c_source_l03962}03962         mid = (start + end) / 2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{vector_8c_source_l03963}03963         \textcolor{comment}{// If number is perfect square}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{vector_8c_source_l03964}03964         \textcolor{comment}{// then break}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{vector_8c_source_l03965}03965         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (mid * mid == number) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{vector_8c_source_l03966}03966             ans = mid;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{vector_8c_source_l03967}03967             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{vector_8c_source_l03968}03968         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{vector_8c_source_l03969}03969         \textcolor{comment}{// Increment start if integral}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{vector_8c_source_l03970}03970         \textcolor{comment}{// part lies on right side}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{vector_8c_source_l03971}03971         \textcolor{comment}{// of the mid}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{vector_8c_source_l03972}03972         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (mid * mid < number) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{vector_8c_source_l03973}03973           \textcolor{comment}{//first start value should be added to answer}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{vector_8c_source_l03974}03974             ans=start;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{vector_8c_source_l03975}03975           \textcolor{comment}{//then start should be changed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{vector_8c_source_l03976}03976             start = mid + 1.;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{vector_8c_source_l03977}03977         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{vector_8c_source_l03978}03978         \textcolor{comment}{// Decrement end if integral part}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{vector_8c_source_l03979}03979         \textcolor{comment}{// lies on the left side of the mid}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{vector_8c_source_l03980}03980         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{vector_8c_source_l03981}03981             end = mid -\/ 1.;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{vector_8c_source_l03982}03982         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{vector_8c_source_l03983}03983     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{vector_8c_source_l03984}03984     \textcolor{comment}{// To find the fractional part}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{vector_8c_source_l03985}03985     \textcolor{comment}{// of square root upto 5 decimal}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{vector_8c_source_l03986}03986     \textcolor{keywordtype}{long} \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} increment = 0.1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{vector_8c_source_l03987}03987     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i = 0; i < 5; i++) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{vector_8c_source_l03988}03988         \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (ans * ans <= number) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{vector_8c_source_l03989}03989             ans += increment;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{vector_8c_source_l03990}03990         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{vector_8c_source_l03991}03991         \textcolor{comment}{// Loop terminates,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{vector_8c_source_l03992}03992         \textcolor{comment}{// when ans * ans > number}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{vector_8c_source_l03993}03993         ans = ans -\/ increment;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{vector_8c_source_l03994}03994         increment = increment / 10;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{vector_8c_source_l03995}03995     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{vector_8c_source_l03996}03996     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} ans;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{vector_8c_source_l03997}03997 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{vector_8c_source_l03998}03998 \textcolor{comment}{// ==========================================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{vector_8c_source_l03999}03999 \textcolor{comment}{// ==========================================================================================}}
